From lofty thrones to depths below, Parasitic rulers faced their woe. Their empire's glory turned to dust, In the echoes of a power unjust.  The parasites fed on the weakened land, Draining life with a relentless hand. But empires built on greed and decay, Are destined to crumble and fade away.  As whispers of rebellion softly rise, The parasites meet their own demise. The people's strength, a force untold, Brings down the empire, once so bold.  The ruins stand as a solemn trace, A cautionary tale of avarice. For empires built on others' pain, Shall crumble, never to rise again.
